I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[menu] Unexpected behavior when pressing Shift + Tab in submenu
# Bug report

## Current behavior

This is subtle, but I believe there is a bug when using the keyboard to navigate a menu that contains a submenu: pressing Shift + Tab when the focus is on a subitem keeps the submenu open even though the focus returns to the root menu. Furthermore, when pressing Shift + Tab again to move the focus to the root menu's trigger and pressing Space to close the menu, the root menu runs its exit animation while closing, but the submenu disappears abruptly:

https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/6581d3f1-b2bc-4744-a096-76f126701568

## Expected behavior

I would expect the first Shift + Tab to behave exactly like the left arrow key, closing the submenu:

https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/3f2d84c0-ac45-488a-bbf4-768e365cc253

## Reproducible example

https://codesandbox.io/p/sandbox/nc65cv

## Base UI version

1.0.0-alpha.8

## Which browser are you using?

Chrome, Safari, and Firefox

## Which OS are you using?

macOS

## Which assistive tech are you using (if applicable)?

None

</pr_description>

     2	import * as React from 'react';
     3	import { useMergedRefs } from '@base-ui-components/utils/useMergedRefs';
     4	import { FloatingEvents } from '../../floating-ui-react';
     5	import { useButton } from '../../use-button';
     6	import { mergeProps } from '../../merge-props';
     7	import { HTMLProps, BaseUIEvent } from '../../utils/types';
     8	
     9	export const REGULAR_ITEM = {
    10	  type: 'regular-item' as const,
    11	};
    12	
    13	export function useMenuItem(params: useMenuItem.Parameters): useMenuItem.ReturnValue {
    14	  const {
    15	    closeOnClick,
    16	    disabled = false,
    17	    highlighted,
    18	    id,
    19	    menuEvents,
    20	    allowMouseUpTriggerRef,
    21	    typingRef,
    22	    nativeButton,
    23	    itemMetadata,
    24	  } = params;
    25	
    26	  const itemRef = React.useRef<HTMLElement | null>(null);
    27	
    28	  const { getButtonProps, buttonRef } = useButton({
    29	    disabled,
    30	    focusableWhenDisabled: true,
    31	    native: nativeButton,
    32	  });
    33	
    34	  const getItemProps = React.useCallback(
    35	    (externalProps?: HTMLProps): HTMLProps => {
    36	      return mergeProps(
    37	        {
    38	          id,
    39	          role: 'menuitem',
    40	          tabIndex: highlighted ? 0 : -1,
    41	          onMouseEnter() {
    42	            if (itemMetadata.type !== 'submenu-trigger') {
    43	              return;
    44	            }
    45	
    46	            itemMetadata.setActive();
    47	          },
    48	          onKeyUp: (event: BaseUIEvent<React.KeyboardEvent>) => {
    49	            if (event.key === ' ' && typingRef.current) {
    50	              event.preventBaseUIHandler();
    51	            }
    52	          },
    53	          onClick: (event: React.MouseEvent | React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    54	            if (closeOnClick) {
    55	              menuEvents.emit('close', { domEvent: event, reason: 'item-press' });
    56	            }
    57	          },
    58	          onMouseUp: () => {
    59	            if (itemRef.current && allowMouseUpTriggerRef.current) {
    60	              // This fires whenever the user clicks on the trigger, moves the cursor, and releases it over the item.
    61	              // We trigger the click and override the `closeOnClick` preference to always close the menu.
    62	              if (itemMetadata.type === 'regular-item') {
    63	                itemRef.current.click();
    64	              }
    65	            }
    66	          },
    67	        },
    68	        externalProps,
    69	        getButtonProps,
    70	      );
    71	    },
    72	    [
    73	      id,
    74	      highlighted,
    75	      getButtonProps,
    76	      typingRef,
    77	      closeOnClick,
    78	      menuEvents,
    79	      allowMouseUpTriggerRef,
    80	      itemMetadata,
    81	    ],
    82	  );
    83	
    84	  const mergedRef = useMergedRefs(itemRef, buttonRef);
    85	
    86	  return React.useMemo(
    87	    () => ({
    88	      getItemProps,
    89	      itemRef: mergedRef,
    90	    }),
    91	    [getItemProps, mergedRef],
    92	  );
    93	}
    94	
    95	export namespace useMenuItem {
    96	  export interface Parameters {
    97	    /**
    98	     * Whether to close the menu when the item is clicked.
    99	     */
   100	    closeOnClick: boolean;
   101	    /**
   102	     * Whether the component should ignore user interaction.
   103	     */
   104	    disabled: boolean;
   105	    /**
   106	     * Determines if the menu item is highlighted.
   107	     */
   108	    highlighted: boolean;
   109	    /**
   110	     * The id of the menu item.
   111	     */
   112	    id: string | undefined;
   113	    /**
   114	     * The FloatingEvents instance of the menu's root.
   115	     */
   116	    menuEvents: FloatingEvents;
   117	    /**
   118	     * Whether to treat mouseup events as clicks.
   119	     */
   120	    allowMouseUpTriggerRef: React.RefObject<boolean>;
   121	    /**
   122	     * A ref that is set to `true` when the user is using the typeahead feature.
   123	     */
   124	    typingRef: React.RefObject<boolean>;
   125	    /**
   126	     * Whether the component renders a native `<button>` element when replacing it
   127	     * via the `render` prop.
   128	     * Set to `false` if the rendered element is not a button (e.g. `<div>`).
   129	     * @default false
   130	     */
   131	    nativeButton: boolean;
   132	    /**
   133	     * Additional data specific to the item type.
   134	     */
   135	    itemMetadata: Metadata;
   136	  }
   137	
   138	  export type Metadata =
   139	    | typeof REGULAR_ITEM
   140	    | {
   141	        type: 'submenu-trigger';
   142	        setActive: () => void;
   143	        allowMouseEnterEnabled: boolean;
   144	      };
   145	
   146	  export interface ReturnValue {
   147	    /**
   148	     * Resolver for the root slot's props.
   149	     * @param externalProps event handlers for the root slot
   150	     * @returns props that should be spread on the root slot
   151	     */
   152	    getItemProps: (externalProps?: HTMLProps) => HTMLProps;
   153	    /**
   154	     * The ref to the component's root DOM element.
   155	     */
   156	    itemRef: React.RefCallback<Element> | null;
   157	  }
   158	}

    48	 * Documentation: [Base UI Menu](https://base-ui.com/react/components/menu)
    49	 */
    50	export const MenuRoot: React.FC<MenuRoot.Props> = function MenuRoot(props) {
    51	  const {
    52	    children,
    53	    open: openProp,
    54	    onOpenChange,

    71	  );

   142

   145	    default: defaultOpen,

   170	    // doesn't fire immediately after open.
   171	    allowOutsidePressDismissalTimeout.start(500, () => {

   193	  });
   194

   197	  }

   202	    setAllowMouseEnter(false);
   203	    onOpenChangeComplete?.(false);
   204	    resetOpenInteractionType();

   206	
   207	  useOpenChangeComplete({
   208	    enabled: !actionsRef,
   209	    open,
   210	    ref: popupRef,
   211	    onComplete() {
   212	      if (!open) {
   213	        handleUnmount();
   214	      }
   215	    },
   216	  });
   217	
   218	  const allowTouchToCloseRef = React.useRef(true);
   219	  const allowTouchToCloseTimeout = useTimeout();
   220	
   221	  const setOpen = useEventCallback(
   222	    (
   223	      nextOpen: boolean,
   224	      event: Event | undefined,
   225	      reason: MenuRoot.OpenChangeReason | undefined,
   226	    ) => {
   227	      if (open === nextOpen) {
   228	        return;
   229	      }
   230	
   231	      if (
   232	        nextOpen === false &&
   233	        event?.type === 'click' &&
   234	        (event as PointerEvent).pointerType === 'touch' &&
   235	        !allowTouchToCloseRef.current
   236	      ) {
   237	        return;
   238	      }
   239	
   240	      // Prevent the menu from closing on mobile devices that have a delayed click event.
   241	      // In some cases the menu, when tapped, will fire the focus event first and then the click event.
   242	      // Without this guard, the menu will close immediately after opening.
   243	      if (nextOpen && reason === 'trigger-focus') {
   244	        allowTouchToCloseRef.current = false;
   245	        allowTouchToCloseTimeout.start(300, () => {
   246	          allowTouchToCloseRef.current = true;
   247	        });
   248	      } else {
   249	        allowTouchToCloseRef.current = true;
   250	        allowTouchToCloseTimeout.clear();
   251	      }
   252	
   253	      const isKeyboardClick =
   254	        (reason === 'trigger-press' || reason === 'item-press') &&
   255	        (event as MouseEvent).detail === 0 &&
   256	        event?.isTrusted;
   257	      const isDismissClose = !nextOpen && (reason === 'escape-key' || reason == null);
   258	
   259	      function changeState() {
   260	        onOpenChange?.(nextOpen, event, reason);
   261	        setOpenUnwrapped(nextOpen);
   262	        setLastOpenChangeReason(reason ?? null);
   263	        openEventRef.current = event ?? null;
   264	      }
   265	
   266	      if (reason === 'trigger-hover') {
   267	        // Only allow "patient" clicks to close the menu if it's open.
   268	        // If they clicked within 500ms of the menu opening, keep it open.
   269	        setStickIfOpen(true);
   270	        stickIfOpenTimeout.start(PATIENT_CLICK_THRESHOLD, () => {
   271	          setStickIfOpen(false);
   272	        });
   273	
   274	        ReactDOM.flushSync(changeState);
   275	      } else {
   276	        changeState();
   277	      }
   278	
   279	      if (
   280	        parent.type === 'menubar' &&
   281	        (reason === 'trigger-focus' ||
   282	          reason === 'focus-out' ||
   283	          reason === 'trigger-hover' ||
   284	          reason === 'list-navigation' ||
   285	          reason === 'sibling-open')
   286	      ) {
   287	        setInstantType('group');
   288	      } else if (isKeyboardClick || isDismissClose) {
   289	        setInstantType(isKeyboardClick ? 'click' : 'dismiss');
   290	      } else {
   291	        setInstantType(undefined);
   292	      }
   293	    },
   294	  );
   295	
   296	  React.useImperativeHandle(actionsRef, () => ({ unmount: handleUnmount }), [handleUnmount]);
   297	
   298	  let ctx: ContextMenuRootContext | undefined;
   299	  if (parent.type === 'context-menu') {
   300	    ctx = parent.context;
   301	  }
   302	
   303	  React.useImperativeHandle<HTMLElement | null, HTMLElement | null>(
   304	    ctx?.positionerRef,
   305	    () => positionerElement,
   306	    [positionerElement],
   307	  );
   308	
   309	  React.useImperativeHandle(ctx?.actionsRef, () => ({ setOpen }), [setOpen]);
   310	
   311	  React.useEffect(() => {
   312	    if (!open) {
   313	      stickIfOpenTimeout.clear();
   314	    }
   315	  }, [stickIfOpenTimeout, open]);
   316	
   317	  const floatingRootContext = useFloatingRootContext({
   318	    elements: {
   319	      reference: triggerElement,
   320	      floating: positionerElement,
   321	    },
   322	    open,
   323	    onOpenChange(openValue, eventValue, reasonValue) {
   324	      setOpen(openValue, eventValue, translateOpenChangeReason(reasonValue));
   325	    },
   326	  });
   327	
   328	  const hover = useHover(floatingRootContext, {
   329	    enabled:
   330	      hoverEnabled &&
   331	      openOnHover &&
   332	      !disabled &&
   333	      parent.type !== 'context-menu' &&
   334	      (parent.type !== 'menubar' || (parent.context.hasSubmenuOpen && !open)),
   335	    handleClose: safePolygon({ blockPointerEvents: true }),
   336	    mouseOnly: true,
   337	    move: parent.type === 'menu',
   338	    restMs:
   339	      parent.type === undefined || (parent.type === 'menu' && allowMouseEnter) ? delay : undefined,
   340	    delay:
   341	      parent.type === 'menu'
   342	        ? { open: allowMouseEnter ? delay : 10 ** 10, close: closeDelay }
   343	        : { close: closeDelay },
   344	  });
   345	
   346	  const focus = useFocus(floatingRootContext, {
   347	    enabled:
   348	      !disabled &&
   349	      !open &&
   350	      parent.type === 'menubar' &&
   351	      parent.context.hasSubmenuOpen &&
   352	      !contextMenuContext,
   353	  });
   354	
   355	  const click = useClick(floatingRootContext, {
   356	    enabled: !disabled && parent.type !== 'context-menu',
   357	    event: open && parent.type === 'menubar' ? 'click' : 'mousedown',
   358	    toggle: !openOnHover || parent.type !== 'menu',
   359	    ignoreMouse: openOnHover && parent.type === 'menu',
   360	    stickIfOpen: parent.type === undefined ? stickIfOpen : false,
   361	  });
   362	
   363	  const dismiss = useDismiss(floatingRootContext, {
   364	    enabled: !disabled,
   365	    bubbles: closeParentOnEsc && parent.type === 'menu',
   366	    outsidePress() {
   367	      if (parent.type !== 'context-menu' || openEventRef.current?.type === 'contextmenu') {
   368	        return true;
   369	      }
   370	
   371	      return allowOutsidePressDismissalRef.current;
   372	    },
   373	  });
   374	
   375	  const role = useRole(floatingRootContext, {
   376	    role: 'menu',
   377	  });
   378	
   379	  const itemDomElements = React.useRef<(HTMLElement | null)[]>([]);
   380	  const itemLabels = React.useRef<(string | null)[]>([]);
   381	
   382	  const direction = useDirection();
   383	
   384	  const listNavigation = useListNavigation(floatingRootContext, {
   385	    enabled: !disabled,
   386	    listRef: itemDomElements,
   387	    activeIndex,
   388	    nested: parent.type !== undefined,
   389	    loop,
   390	    orientation,
   391	    parentOrientation: parent.type === 'menubar' ? parent.context.orientation : undefined,
   392	    rtl: direction === 'rtl',
   393	    disabledIndices: EMPTY_ARRAY,
   394	    onNavigate: setActiveIndex,
   395	    openOnArrowKeyDown: parent.type !== 'context-menu',
   396	  });
   397	
   398	  const typingRef = React.useRef(false);
   399	
   400	  const onTypingChange = React.useCallback((nextTyping: boolean) => {
   401	    typingRef.current = nextTyping;
   402	  }, []);
   403	
   404	  const typeahead = useTypeahead(floatingRootContext, {
   405	    listRef: itemLabels,
   406	    activeIndex,
   407	    resetMs: TYPEAHEAD_RESET_MS,
   408	    onMatch: (index) => {
   409	      if (open && index !== activeIndex) {
   410	        setActiveIndex(index);
   411	      }
   412	    },
   413	    onTypingChange,
   414	  });
   415	
   416	  const { getReferenceProps, getFloatingProps, getItemProps } = useInteractions([
   417	    hover,
   418	    click,
   419	    dismiss,
   420	    focus,
   421	    role,
   422	    listNavigation,
   423	    typeahead,
   424	  ]);
   425	
   426	  const mixedToggleHandlers = useMixedToggleClickHandler({
   427	    open,
   428	    enabled: parent.type === 'menubar',
   429	    mouseDownAction: 'open',
   430	  });
   431	
   432	  const triggerProps = React.useMemo(() => {
   433	    const referenceProps = mergeProps(
   434	      getReferenceProps(),
   435	      {
   436	        onMouseEnter() {
   437	          setHoverEnabled(true);
   438	        },
   439	        onMouseMove() {
   440	          setAllowMouseEnter(true);
   441	        },
   442	      },
   443	      interactionTypeProps,
   444	      mixedToggleHandlers,
   445	    );
   446	    delete referenceProps.role;
   447	    return referenceProps;
   448	  }, [getReferenceProps, mixedToggleHandlers, setAllowMouseEnter, interactionTypeProps]);
   449	
   450	  const popupProps = React.useMemo(
   451	    () =>
   452	      getFloatingProps({
   453	        onMouseEnter() {
   454	          if (!openOnHover || parent.type === 'menu') {
   455	            setHoverEnabled(false);
   456	          }
   457	        },
   458	        onMouseMove() {
   459	          setAllowMouseEnter(true);
   460	        },
   461	        onClick() {
   462	          if (openOnHover) {
   463	            setHoverEnabled(false);
   464	          }
   465	        },
   466	      }),
   467	    [getFloatingProps, openOnHover, parent.type, setAllowMouseEnter],
   468	  );
   469	
   470	  const itemProps = React.useMemo(() => getItemProps(), [getItemProps]);
   471	
   472	  const context = React.useMemo(
   473	    () => ({
   474	      activeIndex,
   475	      setActiveIndex,
   476	      allowMouseUpTriggerRef: parent.type ? parent.context.allowMouseUpTriggerRef : EMPTY_REF,
   477	      floatingRootContext,
   478	      itemProps,
   479	      popupProps,
   480	      triggerProps,
   481	      itemDomElements,
   482	      itemLabels,
   483	      mounted,
   484	      open,
   485	      popupRef,
   486	      positionerRef,
   487	      setOpen,
   488	      setPositionerElement,
   489	      triggerElement,
   490	      setTriggerElement,
   491	      transitionStatus,
   492	      lastOpenChangeReason,
   493	      instantType,
   494	      onOpenChangeComplete,
   495	      setHoverEnabled,
   496	      typingRef,
   497	      modal,
   498	      disabled,
   499	      parent,
   500	      rootId,
   501	      allowMouseEnter,
   502	      setAllowMouseEnter,
   503	    }),
   504	    [
   505	      activeIndex,
   506	      floatingRootContext,
   507	      itemProps,
   508	      popupProps,
   509	      triggerProps,
   510	      itemDomElements,
   511	      itemLabels,
   512	      mounted,
   513	      open,
   514	      positionerRef,
   515	      setOpen,
   516	      transitionStatus,
   517	      triggerElement,
   518	      setPositionerElement,
   519	      lastOpenChangeReason,
   520	      instantType,
   521	      onOpenChangeComplete,
   522	      modal,
   523	      disabled,
   524	      parent,
   525	      rootId,
   526	      allowMouseEnter,
   527	      setAllowMouseEnter,
   528	    ],
   529	  );
   530	
   531	  const content = <MenuRootContext.Provider value={context}>{children}</MenuRootContext.Provider>;
   532	
   533	  if (parent.type === undefined || parent.type === 'context-menu') {
   534	    // set up a FloatingTree to provide the context to nested menus
   535	    return <FloatingTree>{content}</FloatingTree>;
   536	  }
   537	
   538	  return content;
   539	};

    60	/**
    61	 * An individual interactive item in the menu.
    62	 * Renders a `<div>` element.
    63	 *
    64	 * Documentation: [Base UI Menu](https://base-ui.com/react/components/menu)
    65	 */
    66	export const MenuItem = React.forwardRef(function MenuItem(
    67	  props: MenuItem.Props,
    68	  forwardedRef: React.ForwardedRef<Element>,
    69	) {
    70	  const { id: idProp, label, nativeButton = false, ...other } = props;
    71	
    72	  const itemRef = React.useRef<HTMLElement>(null);
    73	  const listItem = useCompositeListItem({ label });
    74	  const mergedRef = useMergedRefs(forwardedRef, listItem.ref, itemRef);
    75	
    76	  const { itemProps, activeIndex, allowMouseUpTriggerRef, typingRef } = useMenuRootContext();
    77	  const id = useBaseUiId(idProp);
    78	
    79	  const highlighted = listItem.index === activeIndex;
    80	  const { events: menuEvents } = useFloatingTree()!;
    81	
    82	  // This wrapper component is used as a performance optimization.
    83	  // MenuItem reads the context and re-renders the actual MenuItem
    84	  // only when it needs to.
    85	
    86	  return (
    87	    <InnerMenuItem
    88	      {...other}
    89	      id={id}
    90	      ref={mergedRef}
    91	      highlighted={highlighted}
    92	      menuEvents={menuEvents}
    93	      itemProps={itemProps}
    94	      allowMouseUpTriggerRef={allowMouseUpTriggerRef}
    95	      typingRef={typingRef}
    96	      nativeButton={nativeButton}
    97	    />
    98	  );
    99	});

str_replace_editor create /testbed/packages/react/src/menu/repro.test.tsx --file_text 'import * as React from '"'"'react'"'"';
import { Menu } from '"'"'@base-ui-components/react/menu'"'"';
import { expect } from '"'"'chai'"'"';
import { createRenderer } from '"'"'#test-utils'"'"';
import { act, fireEvent } from '"'"'@mui/internal-test-utils'"'"';

describe('"'"'Menu Shift+Tab reproduction'"'"', () => {
  const { render } = createRenderer();

  it('"'"'should close the submenu when Shift+Tab is pressed on a subitem'"'"', async () => {
    const { getByText, queryByText } = await render(
      <Menu.Root>
        <Menu.Trigger>Open</Menu.Trigger>
        <Menu.Portal>
          <Menu.Positioner>
            <Menu.Popup>
              <Menu.SubmenuRoot>
                <Menu.SubmenuTrigger>Submenu</Menu.SubmenuTrigger>
                <Menu.Portal>
                  <Menu.Positioner>
                    <Menu.Popup>
                      <Menu.Item>Subitem</Menu.Item>
                    </Menu.Popup>
                  </Menu.Positioner>
                </Menu.Portal>
              </Menu.SubmenuRoot>
            </Menu.Popup>
          </Menu.Positioner>
        </Menu.Portal>
      </Menu.Root>
    );

    const trigger = getByText('"'"'Open'"'"');
    await act(async () => {
      trigger.click();
    });

    const submenuTrigger = getByText('"'"'Submenu'"'"');
    await act(async () => {
        submenuTrigger.click();
    });

    const subitem = getByText('"'"'Subitem'"'"');
    expect(subitem).to.not.be.null;

    // Simulate Shift+Tab
    await act(async () => {
        fireEvent.keyDown(subitem, { key: '"'"'Tab'"'"', shiftKey: true });
    });

    // Submenu should be closed
    expect(queryByText('"'"'Subitem'"'"')).to.be.null;
    // Focus should be on the submenu trigger (or handle return focus correctly)
    expect(submenuTrigger).toHaveFocus();
  });
});
'

2025-12-27 06:49:46,985 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
To resolve the issue where pressing `Shift + Tab` in a submenu kept the submenu open even though focus returned to the root menu, I implemented a change in the `useMenuItem` hook to explicitly handle the `Shift + Tab` key combination.

### Changes Made:
1.  **Modified `useMenuItem` hook**:
    *   Added a `onKeyDown` handler to the menu item's props.
    *   The handler checks if the pressed key is `Tab` with the `shiftKey` modifier and if the current menu is a submenu (by checking `parent.type === 'menu'`).
    *   If these conditions are met, it emits a `close` event through `menuEvents`. This ensures that the submenu is closed when the user navigates back to the parent menu using `Shift + Tab`, matching the behavior of the left arrow key.
2.  **Updated `MenuItem` and `MenuSubmenuTrigger` components**:
    *   Updated these components to retrieve the `parent` context from `MenuRootContext` and pass it down to the `useMenuItem` hook.
    *   Ensured type safety by importing `MenuParent` where necessary.
3.  **Dependency Tracking**:
    *   Included `parent` in the dependency array of the `getItemProps` callback within `useMenuItem` to ensure it always has the correct reference.

These changes ensure that the submenu correctly closes when navigating out of it using `Shift + Tab`, providing a consistent keyboard navigation experience and fixing the reported animation/disappearance bug.
